<h2 style="text-align: center;">Independent service quality survey results<br>
&nbsp;</h2>
</div>




                                </div>

    <div class="c-103-rich-text parbase">


    


<h3>Personal current accounts (GB)</h3>
<p>Published August 2024<br>
</p>
<p>As part of a regulatory requirement, an independent survey was conducted to ask approximately <strong>1,000&nbsp;</strong>customers of each of the&nbsp;<strong>17 largest personal current account providers</strong>&nbsp;if they would recommend their provider to friends and family. The results represent the view of customers who took part in the survey.</p>
<h4>Overall service quality</h4>
<p>We asked customers how likely they would be to recommend their personal current account provider to friends and family.</p>
<h4>Ranking<br>
&nbsp;</h4>
</div>


    
    
    <div class="c-134-adaptive-image parbase">


    

<div class="adaptive-image    ">
    
    
    
    

    
    
    
    <picture>
        <source media="(max-width: 767px)" srcset="/assets/img/bankaccounts/images/cma-gb-results/hx_pca_servicequal_700x400_aug_2024_1.jpg"/>
        <source media="(max-width: 930px)" srcset="/assets/img/bankaccounts/images/cma-gb-results/hx_pca_servicequal_700x400_aug_2024_1.jpg"/>
        <source media="(min-width: 931px)" srcset="/assets/img/bankaccounts/images/cma-gb-results/hx_pca_servicequal_700x400_aug_2024_1.jpg"/>
        
        
        
        
            
        
        
  
  
  
  
  <img class="adaptive-image-img lazy-img" data-src="/assets/img/bankaccounts/images/cma-gb-results/hx_pca_servicequal_700x400_aug_2024_1.jpg" alt="Personal current accounts (GB) Overall service quality survey results.  Ranking 1st place monzo 80%, 2nd place Starling Bank 79%, 3rd place Chase 78%, 4th place first direct 74%, 5th place Nationwide 70%, equal 7th place Halifax 66%" aria-label="Personal current accounts (GB) Overall service quality survey results.     </picture>

    
    
</div>

<h3>Personal current accounts (NI)</h3>
<p>Published August 2024</p>
<p>As part of a regulatory requirement, an independent survey was conducted to ask approximately <strong>500</strong>&nbsp;customers of each of the&nbsp;<strong>11 largest personal current account providers</strong><span style="font-size: 1rem; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: 0px; display: inline !important;">&nbsp;if they would recommend their provider to friends and family. The results represent the view of customers who took part in the survey.</span></p>
<h4>Overall service quality</h4>
<p>We asked customers how likely they would be to recommend their personal current account provider to friends and family.</p>
<h4>Ranking<br>
&nbsp;</h4>

                                <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-12 col-md-12 grid-col  column-1 ">
                                    
                                    

    




    
    
    <div class="c-103-rich-text parbase">


    


<h2 style="text-align: center;"><a id="appfraudrankings"></a>Authorised push payment (APP) scams rankings in 2023</h2>
<p style="text-align: center;">Authorised push payment (APP) scams happen when someone is tricked into transferring money to a fraudster’s bank account. These charts use data given to the Payment Systems Regulator by major banking groups in the UK in 2023. You can read the full report by visiting <a href="https://www.psr.org.uk/app-fraud-data" target="_self" action-type="Default Link" class="positive btn btn-tertiary" data-selector="cta-item-tertiary"><span class="btn-text">www.psr.org.uk/app-fraud-data</span></a></p>
</div>




                                </div>
							
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                            
                        
                    
                
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

</div>

    <div>
        <div class="container-fluid">
            
            <div class="row animate-grid-content">
		        
                
                    
                        
                            
                                
                                <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-6 col-md-6 grid-col  column-1 ">
                                    
                                    

    




    
    
    <div class="c-103-rich-text parbase">


    


<p>Share of APP scams refunded.<br>
This is the proportion of total APP fraud losses that were reimbursed, ranked out of 14 firms.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>
<p><br>
<br>
<br>
</p>

<p>APP scams sent per £million transactions.<br>
This is the amount of money sent from the victim’s account to the scammer, ranked out of 14 firms.<br>
For example, for every £1 million of Halifax, Bank of Scotland &amp; Lloyds Bank transactions sent in 2023, £228 was lost to APP scams.</p>
